27 /* Call this macro repeatedly. After each use, the pixel data can be extracted
28  */
29 
30 #define HEADER_PIXEL(data, pixel) \
31  { \
32  (pixel)[0] = header_data_cmap[data[0]][0]; \
33  (pixel)[1] = header_data_cmap[data[0]][1]; \
34  (pixel)[2] = header_data_cmap[data[0]][2]; \
35  data++; \
36  }
